So when my birthday rolled around this year, this is what I requested. 48 bottles for 40 bucks, including shipping, that's a pretty fabulous deal.<br /><br />I ordered them late in the evening (around 10pm or so) on Monday, July 8 from MissPinkCat. I got my email notification the next day that they had been shipped, and I found my box on my porch today, Saturday, July 13. Incredibly fast shipping, especially considering the shipping cost me nothing. They were shipped in 8 boxes of 6, none were broken, although I think a couple of them had leaked or something; there was polish on the bottle itself. Not a big deal, they were all full.<br /><br />Onto the polishes themselves. They're fabulous. I didn't get a single duplicate, and there's a lot of different colors. I only got one red, which isn't a problem to me, I very rarely wear red. I only got one holo color, which did disappoint me a bit, but it's so gorgeous I can't be angry about it. Lots of chunky glitters (I counted 9) and lots of normal glittery ones. It's a great range of colors, and I definitely couldn't be happier about that. There are about 5 total that I don't really see myself wearing; I've already decided to regift those to the fellow nail polish lovers in my family. I don't find the smell that overwhelming, they just smell like nail polish to me. I was initially disappointed that I only got a hardener, and no top coat, but after applying the hardener to the polish I already had on, I was pleased to discover that it's perfectly clear and can easily be used as a top coat.<br /><br />As for the remover pads, I simply haven't tried them yet, although the scented part is definitely true. They smell nice, for nail polish remover at least.<br /><br />I would definitely, definitely buy this set again.. as long as I was guaranteed to get 48 more colors. If you're considering buying this, it's worth it!<br /><br />Edit: I've had these for a few days now, and tried out several colors as well as the remover.<br /><br />Personally, I like the little remover pads. They don't work as well as advertised, no, but generally I get one hand removed per one pad. They do leave an oily residue behind, but honestly, a quick go-over with a baby wipe took care of that for me. No weird white streaks or anything.<br /><br />As far as the nail polishes themselves go, I am incredibly pleased. They are bright and vibrant, and they're thick enough you could probably get away with one coat. They dried quickly by my standards, less than 5 minutes per coat, regardless of whether I'd put them in front of a fan like normal or not. My only complaint is that the one holo color I received was more of a topcoat than an actual polish, which is incredibly disappointing. As I've said before, the color itself is completely gorgeous, and I'd love to be able to just have that on my nails.<br /><br />As far as chipping goes.. I've used 3 different colors, had them on for at least 24 hours, and the only chipping problems I've had were caused by my own stupidity -- trying to pick food out of my teeth with my nails, for instance. I've showered, done dishes, typed like a maniac, and all around been hard on my nails, and the polish has held up perfectly.<br /><br />I still have no complaints about the smell at all. I've been doing my nails in a small, completely closed off basement room, (no windows, the only ventilation is my a/c duct), and it's not nearly as bad as some other nail polishes I own. I'd assume if someone is sensitive to smells this would bother them, as the smell is kind of strong.<br /><br />All in all, I could be slightly happier with my purchase; I'd have liked more holo colors, and a deeper color to the one I did get, but none of that is enough to lose a star as far as I'm concerned.

Like I said a very minor detail but something that bothered me. The nail polishes removers were completely dry. I recieved these same nail polish removers in the other lot of polishes I mentioned and they were completely dry as well, they come in a flimsy container that I don't see how it could possibly hold liquid (see note in pros about what I did like about the nail polish removers).<br /><br />Overall I am happy with my purchase.
